
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Regular Rank]
AS 
IIF(
    ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])=0
        or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	    or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
    NULL,
	RANK(
		Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
		except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
		[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Regular Rank', FORMAT_STRING='#,##0', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Tied Rank]
as
IIF(
    ([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])=0
        or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	    or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
    NULL,
    (
        [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Regular Rank], 
        GENERATE(
            {
                INTERSECT(
                    {ORDER(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.MEMBERS, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count], BDESC).ITEM(0)} AS FIRSTTIE,
                    {}
                ),
                ORDER(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.MEMBERS, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count], BDESC)
            } AS [OrderedSet2], 
            IIF(
                ({[OrderedSet2].CURRENT AS CURRATTRIB}.ITEM(0),[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]) = ({[OrderedSet2].ITEM([OrderedSet2].CURRENTORDINAL-2) AS PREVATTRIB}.ITEM(0),[Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]),
                IIF(
                    (PREVATTRIB.ITEM(0), [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count]) = (FIRSTTIE.ITEM(0), [Measures].[Diagnosis - Count])
                    ,{FIRSTTIE}
                    ,{PREVATTRIB AS FIRSTTIE}
                ),
                {CURRATTRIB}
            ),
            ALL
        ).ITEM([Measures].[Diagnosis - Count - Regular Rank]-1)
    )
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Tied Rank', FORMAT_STRING='#,##0', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Diagnosis';

                    {ORDER(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.MEMBERS, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Encounter - Unique Count], BDESC).ITEM(0)} AS FIRSTTIE,

                ORDER(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.MEMBERS, [Measures].[Diagnosis - Encounter - Unique Count], BDESC)
            } AS [OrderedSet2], 
            IIF(
                ({[OrderedSet2].CURRENT AS CURRATTRIB}.ITEM(0),[Measures].[Diagnosis - Encounter - Unique Count]) = ({[OrderedSet2].ITEM([OrderedSet2].CURRENTORDINAL-2) AS PREVATTRIB}.ITEM(0),[Measures].[Diagnosis - Encounter - Unique Count]),

                    ,{PREVATTRIB AS FIRSTTIE}

        or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	    or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
    NULL,
    (
        [Measures].[Surgical Case - Count - Regular Rank], 
        GENERATE(
            {
                INTERSECT(
                    {ORDER(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.MEMBERS, [Measures].[Surgical Case - Count], BDESC).ITEM(0)} AS FIRSTTIE,
                    {}
                ),
                ORDER(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.MEMBERS, [Measures].[Surgical Case - Count], BDESC)
            } AS [OrderedSet2], 
            IIF(
                ({[OrderedSet2].CURRENT AS CURRATTRIB}.ITEM(0),[Measures].[Surgical Case - Count]) = ({[OrderedSet2].ITEM([OrderedSet2].CURRENTORDINAL-2) AS PREVATTRIB}.ITEM(0),[Measures].[Surgical Case - Count]),
                IIF(
                    (PREVATTRIB.ITEM(0), [Measures].[Surgical Case - Count]) = (FIRSTTIE.ITEM(0), [Measures].[Surgical Case - Count])
                    ,{FIRSTTIE}
                    ,{PREVATTRIB AS FIRSTTIE}
                ),
                {CURRATTRIB}
            ),
            ALL
        ).ITEM([Measures].[Surgical Case - Count - Regular Rank]-1)
    )
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Tied Rank', FORMAT_STRING='#,##0', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Surgical Case';

CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Surgical Procedure Event - Count - Regular Rank]
AS 
IIF(
    ([Measures].[Surgical Procedure Event - Count])=0
        or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER
	    or Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER is Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER,
    NULL,
	RANK(
		Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.CURRENTMEMBER, 
		except(Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.members, { Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.DEFAULTMEMBER, Axis(1).Item(0).Item(Axis(1).Item(0).Count - 1).Hierarchy.UNKNOWNMEMBER }), 
		[Measures].[Surgical Procedure Event - Count]
	)
)
,VISIBLE=1, DISPLAY_FOLDER='Rank\Regular Rank', FORMAT_STRING='#,##0', ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP='Surgical Procedure Event';
